registeredNames(bool include_disabled = false) {\n   172→    std::vector<absl::string_view> ret;\n   173→\n   174→    ret.reserve(factories().size());\n   175→\n   176→    for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n   177→      if (factory || include_disabled) {\n   178→        ret.push_back(factory_name);\n   179→      }\n   180→    }\n   181→\n   182→ versionedFactories() {\n   200→    using VersionedFactoryMap =\n   201→        absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion>;\n   202→    MUTABLE_CONSTRUCT_ON_FIRST_USE(VersionedFactoryMap);\n   203→  }\n   204→\n   205→  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::string>& deprecatedFactoryNames() {\n   206→    static auto* */\n   215→  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>& factoriesByType() {\n   216→    static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>* factories_by_type =\n   217→        buildFactoriesByType().release();\n   218→\n   219→    return *factories_by_type;\n   220→  }\n   221→\n   222→  static bool& allowDuplicates() {\n   223→    static bool* allow_duplicates = new registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n   231→                              absl::string_view instead_value = \"\") {\n   232→    auto result =   240→    }\n   241→  }\n   242→\n   243→  /**\n   244→   * version is used for registering vendor specific factories that are versioned\n   245→   * independently of Envoy.\n   246→   */\n   247→  static void registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n   248→                              const envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion& version,\n   249→                              absl::string_view instead_value = \"\") {\n   250→    auto result = factories().emplace(std::make_pair(name, &factory));\n   251→    if (!result.second) {\n   252→      ExceptionUtil::throwEnvoyException(\n   253→          fmt::format(\"Double registration for name: '{}'\", factory.name()));\n   254→    }\n   255→    versionedFactories().emplace(std::make_pair(name, If the factory is registered under multiple\n   264→   * (deprecated) names, all the possible names are disabled.\n   265→   */\n   266→  static bool disableFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n   267→    const auto disable = [](absl::string_view name) -> bool {\n   268→      auto it = factories().find(name);\n   269→      if (it != factories().end()) {\n   270→        it->second = nullptr;\n   271→        return true;\n   272→      }\n   273→      return false;\n   274→    };\n   275→\n   276→    // First, find the canonical name for this factory.\n   277→    absl::string_view canonicalName = canonicalFactoryName(name);\n   278→\n   279→    // Next, disable the factory by all its deprecated names.\n   280→    for (const auto& [deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name] : deprecatedFactoryNames()) {\n   281→      if (mapped_canonical_name == canonicalName) {\n   282→        disable(deprecated_name);\n   283→      }\n   284→    }\n   285→\n   286→    // Finally, disable the factory by its canonical name.\n   287→    return disable(canonicalName);\n   288→  }\n   289→\n   290→  /**\n   291→   * Gets a factory by name. 315→    const auto it = deprecatedFactoryNames().find(name);\n   316→    return (it == deprecatedFactoryNames().end()) ? name : it->second;\n   317→  }\n   318→\n   319→  /**\n   320→   * @return true should only occur in a single threaded\n * environment, which is guaranteed by the static instantiation mentioned above.\n *\n * Example lookup: BaseFactoryType *factory =\n * std::sort(ret.begin(), ret.end());\n\n    return ret;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets the current map of factory implementations.\n   */\n  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>& factories() {\n corresponding\n   * factory pointer to null. If the factory is registered under multiple\n   * (deprecated) names, all the possible names are disabled.\n   */\n  static bool disableFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n    const auto disable = [](absl::string_view name) -> bool {\n      auto it = factories().find(name);\n      if (it != factories().end()) {\n        it->second = nullptr;\n        return true;\n      }\n      return false;\n    };\n\n    // First, find the canonical name for this factory.\n    absl::string_view canonicalName = canonicalFactoryName(name);\n\n    // Next, disable the factory by all its deprecated names.\n    for (const auto& [deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name] : deprecatedFactoryNames()) {\n      if (mapped_canonical_name == canonicalName) {\n        disable(deprecated_name);\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Finally, disable the factory by its canonical name.\n    return disable(canonicalName);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets a factory by name.   for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n      UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(factory_name);\n      if (factory == nullptr) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      for (const auto&
